The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka

PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government  Notiﬁ cations
1A - PG 4367 - 1417 (01/2019)
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
SRI  LANKA  INSTITUTE  OF  ARCHITECTS
New Registration and Renewal of Registration of “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” for the 
year 2019/2020 under the Architects Registration Board, established as per the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects (Amendment) 
Act, No. 14 of 1996.
Reference is made to the notes appearing on pages 1A, 2A, 3A, 4A and 5A  of the Gazette (Extraordinary) No. 
1015/19 of Friday, the 20th February, 1998 of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka  with regard to the Registration 
of persons who are eligible to practice Architecture in Sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” 
and “Architectural Licentiates”. The interpretations of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects (Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996 
in the above Gazette Notiﬁ cation will apply in all respects to the list published below.
 The Architects Registration Board of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects as per the functions and powers vested 
upon it by the said Act. of Parliament, has now prepared the list of the “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural 
Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazette for the Year 2019/2020  (01st February 2019  to 31st January, 2020).
The Architects Registration Board directed me to publish the Names, Addresses and Registration Numbers of the 
“Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” who have been registered as given below.
This registration expires on 31st January, 2020.
 I.S.S
ARANAPALA,
 Registrar,
 Architects  Registration  Board.
Sri Lanka Institute of Architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha,
Colombo 07,
22
nd January, 2019
